// File added: plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode(''));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html') && (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html');
} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/000_objects/index.html');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_32();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'd33d86be2d37ea5c7b77f342b235f34d454fa98d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd33d86be2d37ea5c7b77f342b235f34d454fa98d') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd022aa3da1f3f3e9b1f513da7407fb60610f4e00') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_32();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd33d86be2d37ea5c7b77f342b235f34d454fa98d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('action.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: action.php');
	writefile_33();
	if (!is_file('action.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): action.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('action.php') != 'a1f9761b67b8ba9a31a1e8141139e075161b363b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): action.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('action.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of action.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'a1f9761b67b8ba9a31a1e8141139e075161b363b') {
		if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'bf7bfb604c556b0e88bb7be15b869e6ef4d6739d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: action.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('action.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('action.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('action.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_33();
		if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'a1f9761b67b8ba9a31a1e8141139e075161b363b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): action.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index_desktop.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index_desktop.php');
	writefile_41();
	if (!is_file('index_desktop.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index_desktop.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index_desktop.php') != 'ae556adf553c6e62c1ee0e6e46ca3809984fce93') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index_desktop.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index_desktop.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index_desktop.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index_desktop.php') !== 'ae556adf553c6e62c1ee0e6e46ca3809984fce93') {
		if (@sha1_file('index_desktop.php') !== '0e35e72a2cb7cafec7c8b486439f14a4a118bb9c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index_desktop.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index_desktop.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index_desktop.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index_desktop.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_41();
		if (@sha1_file('index_desktop.php') !== 'ae556adf553c6e62c1ee0e6e46ca3809984fce93') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index_desktop.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index_mobile.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index_mobile.php');
	writefile_42();
	if (!is_file('index_mobile.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index_mobile.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index_mobile.php') != '7fec7753b12402248a6ba50923c211ee81d812e4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index_mobile.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index_mobile.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index_mobile.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index_mobile.php') !== '7fec7753b12402248a6ba50923c211ee81d812e4') {
		if (@sha1_file('index_mobile.php') !== '328032af89a79c2c3d56826edb222ed9ce2eae48') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index_mobile.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index_mobile.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index_mobile.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index_mobile.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_42();
		if (@sha1_file('index_mobile.php') !== '7fec7753b12402248a6ba50923c211ee81d812e4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index_mobile.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.css');
	writefile_43();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.css') != '97a33409b4050e6adcdb524daaa49d5b637afba3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== '97a33409b4050e6adcdb524daaa49d5b637afba3') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== 'b3a97a485de3f9091db50396cba02d3cf72f9b05') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_43();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== '97a33409b4050e6adcdb524daaa49d5b637afba3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php') !== 'f5cc829abe43ea6bd2abbadaa80d2f9c9c5ef1a6') {
